< review>
My vehicles have collectively been broken into 5 times in just 6 months. The garage management says they have no culpability and have no plans to increase security, add cameras, etc. After $10,000 in damages and loss, we're looking for other options but finding it nearly impossible in the city.
Some people have even put signs in their windows saying there is nothing in their car worth breaking into for.  It's ridiculous.
Avoid this garage if you value your vehicle and belongings.< /review>

Alright, buckle up, cause this is about to be super detailed....... :)

First off, I'm just so thankful that I chose this specific location. Even though it was an hour drive for me from Stockton, it was absolutely worth going out of my way for, for the amazing experience I got today.

I've seen a couple of the more sour reviews and it shocks me a bit, so if you're new and considering a visit, I'm confident you'll be taken care of. I was nervous as HECK since it's been well over a decade since I last stepped foot in a dental office, but they were ALL so considerate and gentle and caring, which helped to ease the anxiety so much.

I was the 1st patient in at opening (the earlier, the better, IMO). Yadira at the front desk immediately complimented me on my hair and that instantly made me smile and feel comfortable off the bat. Everything was explained clearly as far as what was going to take place for this visit and I only sat to wait for a few minutes before Julissa took me back for some X-rays. She took my temperature, was super chill and got me through that process fairly quickly.

Then, after just a tiny bit of a wait, Lynden (the hygienist, I believe), came over to take a closer look and she was the absolute sweetest!!!! I explained a couple of my concerns and she surprised me with some positive feedback (which literally brought me to tears because I was expecting way worse news).

Next, the doctor (Alix) came over (again, no real wait) and she was so, so kind. She could see I was emotional and showed care right away. It was just a few more minutes of another thorough look-over and she reassured me that everything was going to be okay. She asked if I had any questions and then went on her way after I thanked her!

Julissa then walked me over to Inna's office, where we got into the insurance stuff. Honestly, this portion was the highlight of today's visit. She was SO personable from the start of our conversation that I almost forgot where I was, haha. How can someone make something tedious or boring a good time? I have no clue, but she did. She was like the cherry on top of the whole experience, honestly. We had a great conversation while she efficiently walked me through the details of scheduling and cost and coverage, etc. etc. She got my appointments set in a jiffy, explained how and what needed to happen moving forward, and sent me on my way as a happy gal.

I know I didn't get any work done yet, but for someone who has lost confidence in her smile for a while, I left cheesing over the the good news and the sincere care I already got on visit #1! They didn't treat me any less than for having Denti-Cal. I felt so taken care of and welcomed and I'm excited to come back in for all of my appointments. Haha, who would've thought that I'd be happy to go to a dentist!!? Idk guys, this place is awesome and like I said, I'm super thankful I gave them a shot.

A big, fat thanks to the staff for making my day! You guys rock at what you do + hope you all have the BEST day too ;)< /review>

<Response>None< /Response><pictures>None<//pictures><UserId.>107778414317519975493<//UserId.>< text>
To normalize this review, I will compare with Pieology and Blaze pizza companies, also here in Pasadena. 800 degrees is the slowest of the three, with a positively leisurely pace of pie building, payment, and slicing. This does seem to blend with the decor and atmosphere of the place, heads and shoulders above the deafening roar of fast-food like Blaze or the blinding white, cafeteria space of Pieology. 800 degrees is luxurious, elegant, and romantic. The downstairs secret tables are by far the best environment, actually quiet and secluded. 800 degrees has moved away from the buffet-like price model of all-the-toppings-you-desire for a fixed cost, with each topping adding a little ($1) or a lot ($3) to the price of the pie. However, this has permitted them to also offer extraordinary choices such as fine Italian meats, shrimp, and the like. The flavors are at least as good as Pieology and superior to Blaze, similarly with their chewy, softer crust that leaves the soggy/cracker like Blaze behind. Their dough is wonderfully yeasty, slightly superior to Pieology. All in all, a nice change of pace from Pieology and arguably superior pizza, but for ~30% more money at least. Pieology will remain our go-to delicious pizza hangout, Blaze in a pinch for reliable edible goodness, and 800 degrees for the date-like experience they are clearly targeting. Not great for families with small kids due to the fancier atmosphere.<//text>

<Text>I came here for their Social Media night where they gave free pizza/salad/drink for liking their social media pages.

* Tarfuno Pizza - truffle cheese, garlic, onion and arugula
Delicious. The Truffle was what made it delicious. Their pizzas are pretty big, so I could had shared with someone else... but if you're hungry, this is enough.

Caesar Salad - standard

* Drinks - their drinks machine is AMAZING. You could get any drink you want. Just select on the screen and push. TECHNOLOGY is amazing.

AMBIANCE:

PRICE:[I didn't pay for it but I gauged the price]

La Boulange is great for when you want a high-quality breakfast or lunch quickly.

Breakfast-wise, there are good vegetable tarts, croissants, macaroons, and other pastries that are well worth trying.

Lunch-wise, there are good salads (goat cheese is my go-to) that are relatively low-calorie; they also have decent sandwiches with a sort of french twist.

They have a good atmosphere that is pretty open air and lots of outside tables if you want to people watch.<//review>

Both of the people seated adjacent to me were served in a reasonable period of time: one had ordered eggs, bacon, toast, etc. and the other ordered granola. Meanwhile, no food for me; no server came by to check either. When I inquired about my food a server brought my (now) cold oatmeal to the table, so cold that it had developed a crust on the top.

There was no apologies from the wait staff, no offer of compensation, nothing except a bill.

My recommendation to y'all, stay away from Perry's at SRF Terminal 1 with a 10-ft pole!!!  It's the worst on all accounts!< /text>

< Text>
Went here for a business dinner with some colleagues and was pleasantly surprised. This place is very cute and perfect for groups.

While waiting, we ordered the quesadilla, wings and a bottle of wine (1/2 off on Mondays). Both appetizers were delicious! The dry breadsticks were nice to have, but I'd rather waste my calories on actual breadsticks.

I am unsure of what everybody ordered, but I believe there were:
Cobb Salad - all 3 women thoroughly enjoyed this
Pot Roast - tender, flavorful and very filling
Perry's Hamburger - very generous serving of meat, cooked perfectly
Sliders - looked delicious!

Overall, didn't hear any complaints about the food and atmosphere was great. Would definitely return for dinner again!<//Text>
